[04/09/22, 10:11:04‚ÄØPM] CM Jagdish-CREA(I) VP: *IMPORTANT NOTE & GUIDELINES  - YOUR CREA (I) WHATSAPP / TELEGRAM GROUP POSTINGS* 


For the benefit of our members in particular and the Association in general, we are once again highlighting the guidelines to be strictly followed while posting messages in *Your CREA (I) WhatsApp / Telegram Group.*

1) *TIMINGS FOR POSTINGS*
 _Strictly between 8.00 AM to 9.00 PM._ 

2) *WHAT TO POST*
Only messages related to Real Estate availability and requirements.

 *NO GOOD MORNING/ GOOD NIGHT POSTS AT ALL. NO POSITIVE THOUGHTS / FUN / MOCKERY POSTS/ MESSAGES.* 
 
3) *PHOTOS*
Maximum of 2 photos related to Real Estate inventory. 

4) *VIDEOS*
Please post link to the videos & not the video itself

No photos / videos of Developer Projects as a backdrop or in the interest of promoting their projects as a whole.

*5) CONGRATULATORY MESSAGES*
Please send Congratulatory messages to other members only on their private windows. Let‚Äôs keep this group confined to inventory & requirements only. 

Members are requested to strictly follow the above guidelines and *VIOLATION* of any guideline will invite delisting. 
*First Violation* - 3 days
*Second Violation* - 1 week 
*Third Violation* - Admin to take suitable action

Please follow these Guidelines to help yourself and others to conduct business. 

*We value your membership and commitment to CREA (I). Privileged to have you as a fellow member and colleague.* 

*Warmest Regards*,

*Manager- CREA (I)*
